<userid>101623420882728942390< /userid><name>Jojo N< /name><Date>1589066594937<//Date><Rating>1<//Rating>< Review>
Online order and pickup at this store was really bad. The instructions on the email confirmation tell you to call when you get there and they will then leave your order on the table outside. When we got there, there was a long line of people on one side and another group of people waiting around the door. It was not possible to call in at all. Finally, a member of the staff told us to check in by waiting in line. The other group of people by the door had already checked in and were waiting for their order to be placed on the table. What then is the point of ordering online? The whole ordeal was so chaotic. There was barely any social distancing, everyone was crossing in front of you and at the back of you. They tried to put markings that were six feet apart for the line but the line was so long that it wrapped the entire walkway and back. We saw a member of the staff telling some customers to stand back and not get near the door yet she came in contact with other customers picking up their order. They should designate pick up time slots like other stores.<//Review>

<Name>Robert Perez<//Name>< text>
Not sure why I'm having to write another review about this place but if you want authentic Chinese food you need to come here they serve some very authentic dishes including beef tongue and chicken feet among other things like shumai and Hargow! Delicious! The Authenticity of the food is what really gets them 5 Stars but they're also nice people so makes it a positive and energizing experience especially in these trying times. Get Your self an Order of BBQ Pork Steam Bun! Omg! Delicious! If you like REAL CHINESE FOOD come here but if you like that Americanized version of Chinese Fast Food this is not that this is the real deal. I come here like 4 times a month or once per week it's the closest thing in Authentic Chinese Food from Riverside to L.A.</text>

Big Sky Bistro is great for dim sum and regular dining. The French-style beef is great, and the honey walnut shrimp is magnificent, but there are so many awesome options, it's easy to dine adventurously. We've had excellent dumplings of many kinds, so many different noodle options, great soups, and don't forget the Chinese donuts with condensed milk. They do a great to-go service, too. I highly recommend Big Sky, for Western and Eastern tastes.< /Text>

<Text>We were so excited for a new dim sum place nearby but after 2 hours later, we were very disappointed. The food and quality was actually pretty good, but the service and timing of the food being brought out in a timely manner and absolutely ridiculous. We got there shortly after 11, when they opened. They already had some tables seated but it wasn't too busy just yet. We ordered our food and we had the rice, potstickers and BBQ pork brought out in a reasonable amount of time. The rest of our order, which was the bulk of it came out a little over an hour later! It was so disappointing. No one ever checked on us, we asked for some forks and spoons for the kids and they forgot. Had to get up and get it ourselves. They were clearly understaffed, with all of them running around like crazy and even seemed like 2 of the servers (maybe the older gentleman was a manager) were arguing. As we sat there waiting for our food, the restaurant got busier and busier with customers. Unsure if we'll ever go back, maybe if they get more staff or cooks in the back. Still in search of a traditional dim sum place in the IE that has the carts that come around table to table. Overall food was a 3/4. But service and wait for food was a 1/2 at best.

- Dumplings were good size, quality & taste ( shrimp hargow, pork & shrimp shumai, BBQ pork bun, piggy bun, potstickers)

- BBQ pork, Chinese broccoli with oyster sauce, beef wide rice noodle we're good.

<date>1526453324164< /date><rate>5<//rate>< text>
Came here yesterday around 430pm. the place was empty, there's only a couple people there when we arrived. we were greeted by the manager, told us to sit wherever we like.
mom was craving for siomai but we were told that they only serve that during lunch time. he was like, "you can order it during lunch time", and i said, "but we leave so far", and the manager said, "thats really close, i commute from LA everyday!" my mouth dropped lol.. ok he beat me, but seriously everytime i'm free, there's always traffic on the 60! so my mom got very sad, but the manager pulled it off and told us that he will try making it, (to make my mom happy) i mean after all, there wasnt many people.
this is actually the 2nd time i ate here, it was bomb! shrimp fried rice and the pork chop peking style was really good! tender and soft. the wonton soup with noodles was perfect. i couldnt ask for anything more! the shanghai dumpling was lacking taste, but thats just me.. the siomai was better though.
i also ordered the ice milk tea, it says on the menu it doesnt have any refills, but the manager and waiter kept giving me refills, it was cool!
we still had some leftovers, our bill was $50 for all the plates we ordered. we will definitely come back here again.<//text>

<user_name>Ayisha Gabri< /user_name><time>1456514706484</time>< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< Review>
My family decided to try a Pupuseria while out in L.A. and ended up here.  We were happy to notice it's A grade.  Once inside, we were asked if it was for here or to go.  After being told it was for dining there, we were given 3 menus.  We are a family of 6, so one for me, my husband and oldest child.  Although it started off pleasant, it only went down hill.
We ordered a total of 7 pupusas and 4 meals with side of platano macho/frito (fried bananas).  It was so frustrating when our waitress came with all pupusas at once and couldn't tell us which was which.  She pretty much guessed as she passed them out.  Long story short, in trying to get it all straightened out, an older lady from the back came out to try and help, to only end up making it worse.  The two women were talking over my husband and I while we were trying to explain that we were given the order all mixed up, not all the correct kind and still in need of the two bean and cheese that my daughter had ordered.
Although they were trying hard to be quick to fix it, they would have still gotten it wrong being that they were not listening!  It was horrible and so frustrating!

The food was overall average (one plate being yucca and fried chicharon, with the pork being extremely dry), with our favorite being the drinks, horchata and agua de tamarindo.  But, even considering that, after all the confusion and how they were handling it, it really put a damper on the mood.
It didn't help that our waitress never did tend to us the rest of our meal.
So, with that...we give it 2 stars and wouldn't go back.< /Review>

<text>I've been living here for about 5 months. Overall, I like it. I'd give it a 3.5 stars.

The neighborhood is safe and walkable. The neighbors are quiet and respectful. I get the occasional sports nights or food grilling, but nothing to be obnoxious about.  The maintenance crew is hardworking, down-to-earth, and cool. They're always hustling to keep the place clean. Thank you!

Also, I enjoy grabbing a quick bite  and shopping for home goods without having to drive. Across the street, there's Target, Hobby Lobby, Armadillo Willy Bbq, Chitpotle, Pandas Express, Marshall,  Starbucks, and Home Depot.

Furthermore, I like how the units are organized into gated villas with lots of greenery. The gated parking and bike storage area are awesome, but each unit only gets one reserved carport. There's somewhat of ample public/street parking to make up for it, but I don't know how the parking situation will be post-covid.

HOWEVER.....

1) The sewage bill is ridiculous. I'm getting charged ~$110 a month for a unit of three people. One of us work in the office and the two of us work from home. We probably do our laundry three times a month, dishwasher once/twice a month, and shower once a day. I'm confident we use the sink food shredder and bathroom moderately, but I won't go into details. Thus, there is no reason to be charged the amount for our normal usage.

I talked to Edgar in the office and he  told me the total cost of the whole apartment complex sewage is split across all units equally. So, there's not really an incentive to use bathroom, food waste shredder, and laundry moderately. THIS SUCKS.
